    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'

<span id="freeTextContainer1073159766374078140">He comes to her more dead than alive, a towering black-clad stranger riddled with bullets and rapidly losing blood. As she struggles to save him, veterinarian Tess Culver is unaware that the man calling himself Dante is no man at all but one of the Breed, vampire warriors engaged in a desperate battle.<br/><br/>In a single erotically charged moment, Tess is plunged into his world - </span>
  <span id="freeText1073159766374078140" style="display:none">He comes to her more dead than alive, a towering black-clad stranger riddled with bullets and rapidly losing blood. As she struggles to save him, veterinarian Tess Culver is unaware that the man calling himself Dante is no man at all but one of the Breed, vampire warriors engaged in a desperate battle.<br /><br />In a single erotically charged moment, Tess is plunged into his world - a shifting, shadowed place where bands of Rogue vampires stalk the night, cutting a swath of terror. Haunted by visions of a dark future, Dante lives and fights like there is no tomorrow.<br /><br />Tess is a complication he does not need - but now, with his brethren under attack, he must shield Tess from a growing threat that includes Dante himself. For with one reckless, irresistible kiss, she has become an inextricable part of his underworld realm...and his touch awakens her to hidden gifts, desires, and hungers she never knew she possessed. Bonded by blood, Dante and Tess must work together to thwart deadly enemies, even as they discover a passion that transcends the boundaries of life itself.</span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/1391939-i-have-just-started-reading-this-book-the">I have just started reading this book. The first one reminded me much of DARK LOVER (BDB) series. This one is so much similar to Vicious&#39; story LOVER UNBOUND (BDB) series,it left me reeling. So checked publication dates. As you can see this on was published on 29 MAY 2007 whereas Lover unbound was published on 1 OCT 2007 . I just want to know WHO COPIED WHOM? Lara or JR Ward?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>

<li class='footerItem like'>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I don't think 4 months are enough to steal together an entire look and feel of another book. I believe they are both heavily inspired by the same prev<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I don't think 4 months are enough to steal together an entire look and feel of another book. I believe they are both heavily inspired by the same previous works like BDB as you already pointed out and just came out similarly because of it.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/1591513-is-this-book-a-continuation-of-the-first">Is this book a continuation of the first with Gabrielle and Lucan or is completely separate?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_1591513'><a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F715791.Kiss_of_Crimson">like</a></span>

<a href="/questions/1591513-is-this-book-a-continuation-of-the-first">Add your answer</a>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/81996345-noone"><img alt="" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_100x100-259587f1619f5253426a4fa6fb508831.png" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/81996345-noone">Noone</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">It's a direct chronological continuation of the first but with the warrior Dante and a few new characters as protagonists. All major necessary forekno<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">It's a direct chronological continuation of the first but with the warrior Dante and a few new characters as protagonists. All major necessary foreknowledge is repeated in a few short sentences as soon as it comes up but nuance is lost without knowing the first one. Gabrielle and Lucan are very much in the background in this book.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14052818780739187975"><b>4.5 Destine Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='https://imgur.com/QhaT0w5' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1534140426ra/26119716.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I was glad to see that on this second time around, I still really loved Kiss of Crimson. Dante was just as sexy as I remembered. Chase was just as yummy. This book had some great action, some smokin' hot smexy time, and some very yummy warriors all rolled into one awesome read. Dante and Tess had a great connection. Tess had trust issues and Dante was in fear of the visions he has been seeing his whole life. Both were not looking for a relationship let alone love but they we</span>
  <span id="freeText14052818780739187975" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Destine Stars</b><br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/QhaT0w5" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1534140426ra/26119716.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was glad to see that on this second time around, I still really loved Kiss of Crimson. Dante was just as sexy as I remembered. Chase was just as yummy. This book had some great action, some smokin' hot smexy time, and some very yummy warriors all rolled into one awesome read. Dante and Tess had a great connection. Tess had trust issues and Dante was in fear of the visions he has been seeing his whole life. Both were not looking for a relationship let alone love but they were destine to be mates. Not only did I love Tess and Dante, I really loved Chase. Chase seemed so buttoned up but under all that was a total badass. My heart broke for the pain Chase had to endure over his nephew. Elise seemed sweet but I really liked the peek at Tegan's sense of humor. And Rio my poor broken Rio. He needs his boo boos kissed and made all better! I'm on to the next book. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance fans, especially BDB fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2010">read-in-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=warriors">warriors</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer122727255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2388954518476585603"><b>2011 reread: Edited to 5 stars because DANTE IS SEXY AS HELL!!</b><br/><br/>Kiss of Crimson is another solid read by author Lara Adrian. Dante's story is one of intense passion and love. The chemistry between Dante and Tess is instant and electrifying. From the moment they meet, it is clear from the beginning that they are meant for each other. Adrian does an amazing job at telling Dante's story. <br/><br/>I found that I instantly liked Tess the moment she was introduced. As a private practiced vet, she seems to have m</span>
  <span id="freeText2388954518476585603" style="display:none"><b>2011 reread: Edited to 5 stars because DANTE IS SEXY AS HELL!!</b><br /><br />Kiss of Crimson is another solid read by author Lara Adrian. Dante's story is one of intense passion and love. The chemistry between Dante and Tess is instant and electrifying. From the moment they meet, it is clear from the beginning that they are meant for each other. Adrian does an amazing job at telling Dante's story. <br /><br />I found that I instantly liked Tess the moment she was introduced. As a private practiced vet, she seems to have most of her life in control. However, everything changes when Dante steps into her life. For some reason, Dante has his way of getting through Tess' barriers that she walled up when she was a child. Seeing those walls crumble before her and allowing herself to be vulnerable in front of Dante is a beautiful thing to see. Here she learns to trust others again and herself. <br /><br />And Dante - the wicked, hot vampire that wields the twin malebranche blades. How hot is he? Dante kicks some serious ass in this one and I loved every single moment of it. However, there's also another side of him that is much more vulnerable. These two sides put together make Dante so desirable. He's my favourite warrior yet! <br /><br />Sterling Chase is also introduced in this book. And although I didn't like him at first, he's starting to grow on me more and more. Chase has got his own demons to deal with and I'm really interested to see where Adrian takes him.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2388954518476585603" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I expected a bit more from it, to be frank. <br/>I've read this story numerous times. I don't want something original, but I want the characters to be a bit different than the rest. <span id="freeTextContainer17722870146902920780">This book was a dud. It was boring, there is tons and tons of filler that detracts from the "romance", there are too many clichés and stereotypical romance story moments and it's still too similar in my opinion to JR Ward's Black Dagger Brother Hood series--the difference there being that Ward's is top notch. <br/><br/>The love story between Dante and Tess is not well developed and the vampire world story takes up too much "space" between the brief times the couple make it back together again. Nothing rea</span>
  <span id="freeText17722870146902920780" style="display:none">This book was a dud. It was boring, there is tons and tons of filler that detracts from the "romance", there are too many clichés and stereotypical romance story moments and it's still too similar in my opinion to JR Ward's Black Dagger Brother Hood series--the difference there being that Ward's is top notch. <br /><br />The love story between Dante and Tess is not well developed and the vampire world story takes up too much "space" between the brief times the couple make it back together again. Nothing really happens between them until a good 150 pages into the story even. <br /><br />This is more a paranormal story than a paranormal romance. The story outline on the back cover is very misleading--it's like a movie preview that looks really good but those are the best parts of the 2 hour movie and everything in between is a waste of time. <br /><br />I didn't particularly enjoy Book 1 in the series but Book 2 is certainly worse. <br /><br />I like a good paranormal but not when it copies off every other book out there and rolls it into a weak story.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17722870146902920780" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText7063237925780631878" style="display:none">I enjoyed this second book in Lara Adrian’s Midnight Breed series even more than the first. Dante and Tess meet in her veterinarian clinic when he’s badly injured and needs blood. He’s a vampire. She’s human. I really liked Tess, and her special abilities! Also, this one had a really interesting subplot involving a drug that was being sold on the street and had terrible effects on vampires, and it gave book two that extra zing! Some interesting side characters were introduced that I’m excited to read more about in future books. Glad I discovered this series. <br /><br />Please excuse typos/name misspellings.               <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer417552173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7869358565423061655">I feel so dirty saying this, but I am loving this series! The BDB similarities continue unabashedly, but I can’t not read it. <br/><br/>The second book in the Midnight Breed series tells the story of Dante and Tess. Dante is yet another hot, broody vampire (aren't they all? *dreamy sigh*). Viciously wounded, he is found late one night by Tess, our very likeable heroine, who tries to help him and ends up as a blood source. Too late into the piece, Dante discovers that Tess is actually a breedmate and by dr</span>
  <span id="freeText7869358565423061655" style="display:none">I feel so dirty saying this, but I am loving this series! The BDB similarities continue unabashedly, but I can’t not read it. <br /><br />The second book in the Midnight Breed series tells the story of Dante and Tess. Dante is yet another hot, broody vampire (aren't they all? *dreamy sigh*). Viciously wounded, he is found late one night by Tess, our very likeable heroine, who tries to help him and ends up as a blood source. Too late into the piece, Dante discovers that Tess is actually a breedmate and by drinking from her, he is halfway through completing a blood bond with her. Whoops!!!<br /><br />I really liked the twist on this relationship. Tess is in the dark about what is actually going on for most of the book after having her memory wiped of her first encounter with Dante, but she cannot help but fall for the gorgeously hot but mysterious man that suddenly appears in her life. And I loved watching Dante fall hopelessly in love with Tess and become fiercely and swoonily protective of her. <br /><br />Running alongside the romance is a storyline about young vampires going missing and a drug that turns vampires into Rogues. The Breed boys are joined in their operation by Agent Sterling Chase of the Boston Darkhaven (this would be the ‘Butch’ character). I initially thought Chase was a bit straight-laced for the rest of the boys, but after a very surprising visit to a nightclub, I've gotta say I'm intrigued!! I really like him as an addition to the story, and loved the snarky relationship that he develops with Dante. I’m looking forward to seeing more of him in future books. <br /><br />There is also a bit of a set up for the next book – with the mysteriously dangerous <s>Zsadist</s> Tegan having a bit of a moment with emotionally scarred Elise. Looks like there are going to be many obstacles for the two of them, but I can’t wait to see them get their HEA. <br /><br />The action is good with a few surprises thrown in. There are some very steamy scenes, and quite a bit of swoon. The ending was a bit abrupt, but I expect that the storylines will continue into the next books, so I’m not too concerned. <br /><br />Overall, a great read. I’m looking forward to more!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7869358565423061655" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_49139475" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/49139475" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/49139475?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=medical-profession">medical-profession</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=brotherhood">brotherhood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer49139475" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9739160152496540339">Very good book. I am liking this series more and more. The thing that I like most about this series is the interesting mythology and world-building behind the vampires. It's very dark and gritty, and the violence is in your face when it comes to humans being harmed and murdered. I think that part is almost too much for me. I love a book with intense action and a dark edge, but I do hate to see innocent people dying, and this series has a lot of that.<br/><br/>I didn't really find Dante or Tess very tragic</span>
  <span id="freeText9739160152496540339" style="display:none">Very good book. I am liking this series more and more. The thing that I like most about this series is the interesting mythology and world-building behind the vampires. It's very dark and gritty, and the violence is in your face when it comes to humans being harmed and murdered. I think that part is almost too much for me. I love a book with intense action and a dark edge, but I do hate to see innocent people dying, and this series has a lot of that.<br /><br />I didn't really find Dante or Tess very tragic, although they had issues there were dealing with. I guess not all the characters can be tortured although I certainly wouldn't mind. Dante was a character that I enjoyed reading about, but I can't say I ever fell in love with him. I do feel like Dante and Tess were meant to be together.<br /><br />I liked that Tess was a veterinarian, but I think some aspects of her trade were almost simplified. The truth of the matter is that a veterinarian needs lots of help to run her practice. I was wondering how she was accomplishing all the treatment of animals and the money part with just one part-time employee. I'd like to see her give a pet intravenous medications or fluids by herself. Not an easy thing to accomplish. I was glad she didn't romanticize the economic aspects of veterinary medicine. You cannot afford to treat and save every animal and get all the bills paid. It breaks my heart, but I know that this is real life. Tess made choices to price things where she could help the most clients and their pets, but she couldn't make ends meet when it came down to it. This is one of the most heartbreaking aspects of the profession. All and all, it was nice to see a veterinarian doing her thing in these books. <br /><br />I really liked Chase's character although I did not like Elise. She was a bit too whiny-mopey for me. I hope that he moves on from her and finds a real woman who's not so much of a whiny baby. Normally I don't mind a vulnerable heroine, but she bugged me. Probably because she didn't show Chase very much respect as the brother of her dead mate or see him as a flesh and blood man of merit and realize all the sacrifices he had made for her.<br /><br />The part with Rio choked me up. Poor baby. Really looking forward to reading his book. I enjoyed reading scenes with the likable Gideon and his mate Savannah. Nice to see some ethnic diversity in the paranormal romance genre. <br /><br />So all in all, I liked this one more than the first book, and I suspect I will like the books increasingly as the series continues. By the way, just loved little doggie, Harvard. I was so glad he was doing alright. That part nearly made me cry (with some of the stuff going on in my personal life.)</span>
  <a data-text-id="9739160152496540339" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1813695102807681798">Okay, I'll get some heat for this, but though I'm not particularly fond of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/704043.Kiss_of_Midnight__Midnight_Breed___1_' title='Kiss of Midnight (Midnight Breed, #1) by Lara Adrian' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kiss of Midnight</a> (the first book in this series), this one was worse.   <span id="freeText1813695102807681798" style="display:none">Okay, I'll get some heat for this, but though I'm not particularly fond of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/704043.Kiss_of_Midnight__Midnight_Breed___1_" title="Kiss of Midnight (Midnight Breed, #1) by Lara Adrian" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Midnight</a> (the first book in this series), this one was worse. It was slow, extremely déjà vu-ish in parts, I disliked the heroine, could never really warm up to the hero, it was slightly repetitive, etc. I could go on and on, but I'll be concise. It lacked substance to me for some reason, it was generic, and bland, while I expected more from the second book in a series, after the whole world-building is done. Unfortunately, I ended up disappointed. I have high hopes for Tegan's story, though. Keeping my fingers crossed.</span>

<div id="review_953003717" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/953003717" />
    <a title="Lover of Romance" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3709091-lover-of-romance"><img alt="Lover of Romance" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458253423p2/3709091.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/953003717?book_show_action=true">May 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lover of Romance" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lover of Romance" href="/user/show/3709091-lover-of-romance">Lover of Romance</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3709091-lover-of-romance?shelf=genre-paranormal">genre-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3709091-lover-of-romance?shelf=characters-vampire">characters-vampire</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer953003717" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2258194143891169380">This review was originally posted on<a href='http://addictedtoromance.org/2015/09/06/book-review-kiss-of-crimson/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'> Addicted To Romance</a><a href='http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/My-Review.png' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550580i/16122369.png' alt='My Review' width='200' height='67' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/> <br/> 
  <em>
    <strong>Summary </strong>
  </em>
 <br/>Dante, a member of the breed warriors, is out on a night of hunting rogues. Through a series of events, he ends up chasing a rogue, a rogue that is more dangerous than any he has encountered. Harder to kill, suffering from a  bloodlust madness that even regular rogues don't even suffer from. He ends up being shot and he comes across a veterinarian doctor, Tess, who he realizes after the fact of creating a bond to </span>
  <span id="freeText2258194143891169380" style="display:none">This review was originally posted on<a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/2015/09/06/book-review-kiss-of-crimson/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> Addicted To Romance</a><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/My-Review.png" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550580i/16122369.png" alt="My Review" width="200" height="67" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <br> 
  <em>
    <strong>Summary </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Dante, a member of the breed warriors, is out on a night of hunting rogues. Through a series of events, he ends up chasing a rogue, a rogue that is more dangerous than any he has encountered. Harder to kill, suffering from a  bloodlust madness that even regular rogues don't even suffer from. He ends up being shot and he comes across a veterinarian doctor, Tess, who he realizes after the fact of creating a bond to her, that she is a breedmate. Now she is his but only if he can protect her from the danger of his world. Tess has a talent and a heart for connecting with lost animals, and even though financially she is struggling she will do anything to help those in need. She is drawn to Dante, who is dangerous and makes her blood heat. She senses a connection between them, but there are so many secrets surrounding Dante. But when one of her two closest friends gets involved in some dangerous business with the rogues, with young Breeds turning rogue over the drug "Crimson" soon Tess will have to choose between a old friend and the man she is growing to love. Soon Dante and Tess will be thrown into the fire of danger, passion, and betrayal...<br> 
  <em>
    <strong>The Hero </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Dante, is one of the Breed Warriors, and fights to protect both his kind and humans from the savagery of Rogues and their vicious appetites. What I found most intriguing about Dante was his fierce need to protect others. Dante doesn't believe that he will ever be good enough to be lucky to have a mate of his own. He lives to fight and to kill the enemy. Dante's gift is having visions of a future of death and fire...a death he knows will be his and soon. The same happened to his parents, and he knows he inherited his gift from them. Dante is on a mission, to find out the source of Crimson and destroy it. A dangerous drug that turns a breed into a rogue fast...faster than he has ever seen. Their enemy is at work against them once more. Dante is quite the hero in the story. I really loved his fighting spirit and how far he is willing to go to protect the innocent. I really admired Dante because of the way he wins over Tess.<br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <strong>“You would quit the Order for her? Niko asked, the youngest only behind Dante, and a warrior who relished his duty perhaps even more than Dante had himself.</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>I would quit breathing for her, if she asked it of me.”</strong>
  </em>
</blockquote><br>It's not a instant love, it's more he takes his time for her, trying to gain her trust not only for information but also because he is connected to her in an emotional and physical way.<br> 
  <em>
    <strong>The Heroine </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Tess Culver works as a Veterinarian. She connects with animals and they trust her instantly. Tess grew up in a home of a dysfunctional family, where drinking and abuse were apparent. One night haunts her, the night she used her gift, a gift she views as a curse. She left home and built a new life for herself. But to this day, it still haunts her, so she focuses all of her attention on those animals that need her help that come from abusive situations.<br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <strong>“You don’t think I’m . . . some kind of monster? That I’m not much better than him to have killed him like I did, in cold blood?”</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>“Never.” Dante lifted her chin on the edge of his hand. “I think you’re courageous, Tess. An avenging angel, that’s what I think.”</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>“I’m a freak.”</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>“No, Tess, no.” He kissed her tenderly. “You’re amazing.”</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>“I’m a coward. Just like you said, I always ran away. It’s true. I’ve been afraid and running for so long, I’m not sure I can ever stop.”</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>“Then run to me.” Dante’s eyes were fierce as he held her gaze</strong>
  </em>
</blockquote><br>When Tess helps a stranger who is shot, she never realized how her life would be changing. What I liked most about this heroine was her drive. She was dedicated but a bit of a loner. Due to her gift, and her past, she struggles with trust. I really admired her strength and courage, and she proves herself in more ways than one. From beginning to end, we see more facets to her character, and with each chapter you begin to like her more and more.<br> 
  <em>
    <strong>Plot and Story Line </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Kiss of Crimson continues off pretty quickly after Kiss Of Midnight. What I found most enjoyable was seeing Dante and Tess come together in the story. Its not a insta love story, which I was pretty glad about. It takes time, and its done slowly and gradually and I felt so at ease with their romance. This story sets off with a mystery and a dangerous situation of a new drug "Crimson" now this stuff is pretty bad ass, it pretty much destroys a Breed within minutes of inhaling the stuff and turns them into a blood crazed rogue, with superior strength moe than the regular breed and it takes a lot to kill them. This aspect of the story was heartwrenching at times. Because these are young Breeds in their late teens or early twenties who are being destroyed by this drug. We have a side plot of a new character Chase and his secret agenda to find his nephew who has been missing for two weeks. We have Elise, a woman his brother was mated to, but a woman he has loved secretly but knows he will never have a chance with. Even though Chase starts off with secret intentions, they are good ones to save his kin and I respect that. It was just the icing on the cake to see Chase win over the warriors here, despite the lies and deceit, he proves himself capable. We some other character Gideon and Savannah, Lucan and Gabrielle, and poor Rio!! Zero trust with women (which for those who have read the first book, know why) and is scarred and still healing from what happened in the previous book. The love story between Dante and Tess is real and vivid in emotion and passion. They fight for the love they have found together and it is quite moving when they finally trust fully in each other.<br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <strong>“Everything makes sense when I’m with you, Tess. My life makes sense, after so many years of running scared in the dark. You are the light, the reason I live. I’m bonded to you deep, woman. For me, there will never be another.”</strong>
  </em>
</blockquote><br>This book really grabbed my attention, and i stayed up reading because I was so immersed in the story. I love the way Lara Adrian's writing is so compelling and wraps around you like a heated blanket in the dead of winter.<br> 
  <em>
    <strong>The Cover </strong>
  </em>
 <br>I really love the blue and red contrast here...with the red splashes of the city and the blue of the couple. Has an edge and passionate feel to it.<br> 
  <em>
    <strong>Overall View </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Kiss of Crimson is a tantalizing read that sinks its hooks into the reader from the first page. A stimulating page turner that is packed with sizzling passion, edgy suspense, and a mystery to unravel!! THRILLING TO THE END!<br><br><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/Series-Order1.png" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550580i/16122370.png" alt="Series Order" width="200" height="67" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <br><br><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/Kiss-Of-Midnight.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550580i/16122371.jpg" alt="Kiss Of Midnight" width="92" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/Kiss-of-Crimson.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550580i/16122372.jpg" alt="Kiss of Crimson" width="91" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/Midnight-Awakening.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550580i/16122373.jpg" alt="Midnight Awakening" width="91" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/Midnight-Rising.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550580i/16122375.jpg" alt="Veil of Midnight" width="91" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/Ashes-of-Midnight.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550580i/16122376.jpg" alt="Ashes of Midnight" width="91" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_104558525" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/104558525" />
    <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583236251p2/3575839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/104558525?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781849011075" href="/book/show/6512192-kiss-of-crimson">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=va-va-voom-vampires">va-va-voom-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer104558525" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13283487041631000830"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>This is the second in the Midnight Breed series and this time it focuses on Dante, a dark and intense warrior that you meet in the first book and Dr Tess Culver, a vet, they meet accidently (or maybe in a twist of fate) when Dante stumbles into her clinic injured after being attacked by a strange Rogue, he is in need of blood and doesn’t see her Breedmate mark until too late.<br/><br/>I thought this book was an improvement on the first in the series, found the story more engaging and also the cha</span>
  <span id="freeText13283487041631000830" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br /><br />This is the second in the Midnight Breed series and this time it focuses on Dante, a dark and intense warrior that you meet in the first book and Dr Tess Culver, a vet, they meet accidently (or maybe in a twist of fate) when Dante stumbles into her clinic injured after being attacked by a strange Rogue, he is in need of blood and doesn’t see her Breedmate mark until too late.<br /><br />I thought this book was an improvement on the first in the series, found the story more engaging and also the characters more likable. However, although I definitely enjoyed this book more than the first, I thought that Tess and Dante were pretty flat characters, and the love story pretty unbelievable, I think you can count on one hand the amount of times that actually met before them declaring their undying love for one another, and although I read, and like a lot of fated mates books, for some reason I just didn’t buy it, I almost felt like I was missing a vital scene between them or something. <br /><br />However what I did enjoy about this book was Agent Sterling Chase, a detective from the Darkhaven community who comes to the Breed warriors as a lot of youths are disappearing. His character was interesting and seemed far more complex then the two main characters and I look forward to seeing what Ms. Adrian does with him. I also liked seeing some of the other Breed warriors, especially Rio, as you see the consequences of him Breedmate’s actions. However, the relationships between the warriors still seem to lack the camaraderie that I would have expected and although their interactions are shown a bit more it seemed forced. <br /><br />I also enjoyed the continuation of the war between the Breed and the Rogues and how it seems to have stepped up a gear. I like the fact that the adversary in this series is themselves or those that they love and that anyone could turn just by taking a sip too much blood, I think it adds tension to the books. <br /><br />This book was definitely an improvement and although I wasn’t too impressed by the main storyline I did enjoy the new characters introduced and the continued development of the world the Ms Adrian has created. I am going to read on and hope that the next couple will hold my interest more, although I believe the next couple is Elise and Tegan, and I confess to finding Elise slightly irritating in this book, so fingers crossed that she will improve.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13283487041631000830" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_673988548" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="BleuBelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21818379-bleubelle"><img alt="BleuBelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604586298p2/21818379.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/673988548?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="BleuBelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="BleuBelle" href="/user/show/21818379-bleubelle">BleuBelle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=hero-not-celibate">hero-not-celibate</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=not-my-style">not-my-style</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=man-whore">man-whore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=i-don-t-care">i-don-t-care</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=makes-me-angry">makes-me-angry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=it-s-not-for-me">it-s-not-for-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=other-women-men-since-knowing-each">other-women-men-since-knowing-each</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=not-my-kind-of-hero">not-my-kind-of-hero</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer673988548" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1322125383887652727">So I re-read this after 5 years and this was a mistake. My rating went from 5 stars to 1. So, yeah.<br/><br/>I didn't like the Hero. Such a manwhore. After biting and drinking blood from the Heroine (which saved his life!) he saw her tattoo that marked her as a special woman, whom he now was bound to. Eternally. He then wipes her memories. Hero doesn't want or need a woman in his life. And instead of protecting her (she and her kind were hunted by the bad guys and respected and protected by the good guys)</span>
  <span id="freeText1322125383887652727" style="display:none">So I re-read this after 5 years and this was a mistake. My rating went from 5 stars to 1. So, yeah.<br /><br />I didn't like the Hero. Such a manwhore. After biting and drinking blood from the Heroine (which saved his life!) he saw her tattoo that marked her as a special woman, whom he now was bound to. Eternally. He then wipes her memories. Hero doesn't want or need a woman in his life. And instead of protecting her (she and her kind were hunted by the bad guys and respected and protected by the good guys) he leaves her and spends the night with 2 willing woman.<br />I know they aren't dating, they don't even know each other. But Heroine saved his life and they are bonded (on his side) for the rest of their lives. The least he could do is to tell her about herself and protect her.<br /><br />Then there's a lot of back and forth. More memory-scrubbing. Then he becomes jealous of her ex-boyfriend. And all the lying. It isn't until the very end that he tells her he's a vampire. What a prick.<br /><br />Heroine on the other hand had such bad luck with men. Her ex-boyfriend and now friend (really?) is a drug dealer. And she loves him like a brother. Heroine knows he's in love with her, but she decides to go on a date with him, stringing him along. Super sweet of her.<br />I found her really stupid. Goes to find her ex-boyfriend (a known drug dealer) and wants to talk to him, because she gave him the brush-off. Now she feels really sad and wants to make it up to him. What a doormat.<br /><br />I had enough of the manwhore Hero and inexperienced/unfulfilled/unlucky love Heroines.<br /><br />They aren't a couple until the very end. So, I regretted my re-read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1322125383887652727" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition 9781849018692" href="/book/show/16065882-kiss-of-crimson">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18893013-claire?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2298714396" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2416263075849010975"><b> 4 solid stars</b><br/><br/>I liked this book more than the first in this series. Both MCs worked better for me individually AND as a couple, and the pace of the story was faster and never dragging both on the plot and the romance sides. <br/>Definitely going on with the series.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_51115268" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/51115268" />
    <a title="LibraryLass" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/882302-librarylass"><img alt="LibraryLass" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577842488p2/882302.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/51115268?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="LibraryLass" class="user" itemprop="url" name="LibraryLass" href="/user/show/882302-librarylass">LibraryLass</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/882302-librarylass?shelf=library-book">library-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/882302-librarylass?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/882302-librarylass?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/882302-librarylass?shelf=2010">2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/882302-librarylass?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer51115268" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17162956537287220456">The second in what is shaping up to be a fantastic series for me. <br/><br/>I have been off the paranormal kick for a few weeks.... kickstarted again this month with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6289920.Covet__Fallen_Angels___1_' title='Covet (Fallen Angels, #1) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>Covet</a> and now have read this one. I have stayed away from reading both this and the BDB series at the same time because of all the negative comparisons from other reviewers. So I wanted to be able to give this series a chance to stand on its' own merits. So I will read this series first then the BDB.<br/><br/> I loved this one! Both Dante and Tess were</span>
  <span id="freeText17162956537287220456" style="display:none">The second in what is shaping up to be a fantastic series for me. <br /><br />I have been off the paranormal kick for a few weeks.... kickstarted again this month with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6289920.Covet__Fallen_Angels___1_" title="Covet (Fallen Angels, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Covet</a> and now have read this one. I have stayed away from reading both this and the BDB series at the same time because of all the negative comparisons from other reviewers. So I wanted to be able to give this series a chance to stand on its' own merits. So I will read this series first then the BDB.<br /><br /> I loved this one! Both Dante and Tess were great. They had just the right balance of vulnerability and strength, angst and kicka**ness (is that is even a word). The sex was hot, hot, hot! The relationship built at just the right momentum even though I thought I may be put off by how fast Dante 'latched' on to Tess - it didn't put me off in the slightest. Loved all the other characters and like other reviewers I sincerely hope Sterling Chase gets his own story (although looking at the blurbs for all up to Breeds #8 he hasn't so far :( )<br /><br />My only slight grumble is that the climax of the story seemed to be a bit rushed and Tess accepting Dante and his world just a wee bit too slick. I don't know, I guess I'm just a sucker for the hero having to work a bit harder to be accepted and the heroine being a bit more reluctant.<br /><br />Overall, though IMO, it well deserves its' 5 stars from me cos, I finished the book smiling.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17162956537287220456" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/89349845" />
    <a title="Zeek" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek"><img alt="Zeek" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339154824p2/2478293.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/89349845?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zeek" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zeek" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek">Zeek</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=favorites-pnr">favorites-pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer89349845" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13863564970727647036">Dante is part of an elite cadre of warriors whose job it is to keep rogue members of his vampire race in check. When a night out on the town goes awry, he finds himself at Tess Culver's place of business- wounded and in dire need of blood.<br/><br/>Tess has no idea the type of creature that has broken into her veterinary clinic, but she knows he needs help. In one stunning erotic, moment, her life turns upside down, linking her to the stranger for all eternity.<br/><br/>Dante wants to forget the beautiful stranger </span>
  <span id="freeText13863564970727647036" style="display:none">Dante is part of an elite cadre of warriors whose job it is to keep rogue members of his vampire race in check. When a night out on the town goes awry, he finds himself at Tess Culver's place of business- wounded and in dire need of blood.<br /><br />Tess has no idea the type of creature that has broken into her veterinary clinic, but she knows he needs help. In one stunning erotic, moment, her life turns upside down, linking her to the stranger for all eternity.<br /><br />Dante wants to forget the beautiful stranger who saved his life, but fate has made her his and when a strange drug hits the streets turning normally placid members of his race into raging lunatics, he's alarmed to find out she is somehow in the middle of it. <br /><br />Danger and passion infuse their every encounter, as Dante's soul- perhaps for the first time in his long life- awakens from a deep slumber and he discovers Tess is the one woman whom he was meant to protect ... and make his own.<br /><br />Although I enjoyed the first book in this series, I wasn't so enthused with this one. I couldn't get a handle on why we should even like Dante, despite his tortured soul, and I never really felt the connection between him and his fated mate.<br /><br />2 out of 5 from me. I hope the next offering (Tegan's story) will redeem the series for me...</span>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CxHxVtursz2BUYmkA8WjuBm/qRAZT4gdcenJ8I4P2qExN5iEYPV6VSZ6PcX0MKlnz+BO2NfCBnoql49BQ0woOw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UDuTD31tbbc3T2o8+dgPk8pdSlKLjCS1AlAVkvs0tytqHfrdxjOk35Bk3l0OLQVMHAKtmkUBqtJZLlMjNndFsQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2109283127755035384"><b>LARA ADRIAN</b> is a <i>New York Times</i> and #1 internationally best-selling author with nearly 4 million books in print and digital worldwide and translations licensed to more than 20 countries. Her books have been named among Amazon’s Top Ten Romances of the Year, and have also been nominated by readers multiple times as finalists for the Goodreads Choice Award for Best Romance of the Year. Reviewers hav</span>
  <span id="freeText2109283127755035384" style="display:none"><b>LARA ADRIAN</b> is a <i>New York Times</i> and #1 internationally best-selling author with nearly 4 million books in print and digital worldwide and translations licensed to more than 20 countries. Her books have been named among Amazon’s Top Ten Romances of the Year, and have also been nominated by readers multiple times as finalists for the Goodreads Choice Award for Best Romance of the Year. Reviewers have called Lara’s books “addictively readable” (Chicago Tribune), “extraordinary” (Fresh Fiction), “strikingly original” (Booklist), and “one of the best vampire series on the market” (Romantic Times).<br /> <br />Writing as <b>TINA ST. JOHN</b>, her historical romances have won numerous awards including the National Readers Choice; Romantic Times Magazine Reviewer’s Choice; Booksellers Best; and many others. She was twice named a Finalist in Romance Writers of America’s RITA Awards, for Best Historical Romance (White Lion’s Lady) and Best Paranormal Romance (Heart of the Hunter). More recently, the German translation of Heart of the Hunter debuted on Der Spiegel bestseller list.<br /><br />With an ancestry stretching back to the Mayflower and the court of King Henry VIII, the author lives with her husband in New England, where she is working on her next novel. Visit Lara’s website and sign up for new release announcements at <a href="http://bit.ly/LaraAdrianNews" rel="nofollow noopener">http://bit.ly/LaraAdrianNews</a><br /></span>
